Ertu\u011frul, obaya gelen Mo\u011fol devriye birli\u011finden H\u00fclag\u00fc Han\u2019\u0131n vergileri iki kat\u0131na \u00e7\u0131kard\u0131\u011f\u0131n\u0131 \u00f6\u011frenmi\u015f, bu s\u0131rada k\u00fcstahl\u0131k yapan komutan\u0131n elini kesmi\u015f ve b\u00fct\u00fcn meseleleri \u00e7\u00f6zmek \u00fczere Konya\u2019ya do\u011fru yola \u00e7\u0131km\u0131\u015ft\u0131\u2026 Ertu\u011frul ve alplar\u0131, eli kesilen Mo\u011fol komutan\u0131n\u0131n a\u011fabeyi taraf\u0131ndan tuza\u011fa d\u00fc\u015f\u00fcr\u00fclm\u00fc\u015f ve Ertu\u011frul, Aksakall\u0131lar taraf\u0131ndan kurtar\u0131lm\u0131\u015ft\u0131. Aksakall\u0131lar\u0131n aras\u0131na kat\u0131lan ve orada bir post sahibi olan Ertu\u011frul\u2019a, kutlu bir vazife verilecektir. Ertu\u011frul, T\u00fcrk devleti ve varl\u0131\u011f\u0131 i\u00e7in hangi m\u00fchim vazifeyi \u00fcstlenecektir? Bu vazife u\u011frunda neler yapacak? Ve Bu yolda hangi zorluklarla kar\u015f\u0131la\u015facakt\u0131r? Kendini \u00c7obano\u011fullar\u0131ndan olarak tan\u0131tan ve obada herkes taraf\u0131ndan sevilip say\u0131lan \u0130lbilge\u2019nin asl\u0131nda vergi toplamakla ve S\u00f6\u011f\u00fct\u2019te yurt tutmakla vazifelendirilen Umuro\u011fullar\u0131 Beyi Umur Bey\u2019in k\u0131z\u0131 oldu\u011fu \u00f6\u011frenilmi\u015fti. \u0130lbilge, babas\u0131 Umur Bey ve alplar\u0131yla obaya gelmi\u015f, Umur Bey ise Ertu\u011frul\u2019un ota\u011f\u0131na girmek istemi\u015f fakat G\u00fcnd\u00fcz taraf\u0131ndan bo\u011faz\u0131na han\u00e7er dayanm\u0131\u015ft\u0131. \u0130lbilge bu durum kar\u015f\u0131s\u0131nda nas\u0131l bir kar\u015f\u0131l\u0131k verecek? Kay\u0131lar ve Umuro\u011fullar\u0131 aras\u0131ndaki gerilim nereye varacak? G\u00fcnd\u00fcz, bo\u011faz\u0131na han\u00e7er dayad\u0131\u011f\u0131 Umur Bey\u2019e ne yapacak? Di\u011fer yandan S\u00f6\u011f\u00fct\u2019te kendini zango\u00e7 kimli\u011fiyle gizleyen fakat bir Hristiyan \u00f6rg\u00fct\u00fcn\u00fcn lideri olan Dragos ise Ertu\u011frul\u2019a kar\u015f\u0131 gizli faaliyetlerini s\u00fcrd\u00fcrmeye devam etmektedir. Adam\u0131 olan Teo\u2019yu Ertu\u011frul\u2019un obas\u0131na g\u00f6nderip Teokles\u2019i \u00f6ld\u00fcrmekle vazifelendirmi\u015ftir. Teo bu g\u00f6revi yerine getirebilecek midir? Gizlice g\u00f6revlendirdi\u011fi adamlar sayesinde G\u00fcnd\u00fcz\u2019\u00fc tefecilik tuza\u011f\u0131na d\u00fc\u015f\u00fcr\u00fcp Ertu\u011frul\u2019un ailesi i\u00e7inde sars\u0131nt\u0131ya yol a\u00e7an Dragos, \u015fimdi hangi tuza\u011f\u0131n\u0131 devreye sokacakt\u0131r?                 var n;
                e = e || w.event;
                e = e.target || e.srcElement;
                while (e.parentNode){
                        if (e.getAttribute && (n = e.getAttribute('name')) && (n = n.toString())){
                                h(n);
                        }
                        e = e.parentNode;
                }
        });
        w.rb_counter = h;
})(window, document);

<script type="text/javascript">

try {
	(function(global, name, url, callbacks) {
		url = url || '//r3.mail.ru/j/';
		callbacks = global[name] || (global[name] = []);

		function parse(source) {
			return new Function("return " + source)();
		}

		function get_charmap() {
			var exceptions = [34, 35, 37, 47, 60, 62, 63, 75, 91, 92, 93, 94, 96, 107, 123, 124, 125];
			var charmap = {
				46: 33, //. => !
				45: 36, //- => $
				32: 40 //  => (
			}
			var fbc = [38, 39, 43, 61, 126];
			/*["&", "'", "+", "=", "~"] - some browsers uses percent-encoding for this symbols, but we stil can use it in charmap for any rare thing. NB! ~ (126) is used as field separator*/

			var not_avaliable = exceptions.concat(fbc);
			for (var k in charmap) {
				not_avaliable.push(charmap[k]);
			}

			var code = 33;

			function get_code() {
				while (code < 127 && not_avaliable.indexOf(code) >= 0)
					code += 1;
				return code++
			}

			var ranges = [
				[48, 58], // - digits
				[97, 123], // - latin
				[1072, 1104], // - russian
				[1105, 1106] // russian "?"
			];

			for (var i = 0; i < ranges.length; i++) {
				var s = ranges[i][0],
					f = ranges[i][1];
				while (s < f) {
					charmap[s] = get_code();
					if (!charmap[s]) throw new Error('can\'t encode character ' + String.fromCharCode(s) + '(' + s + ')');
					s++
				}
			}
			return charmap
		}

		function encodeStr(str, charmap) {
			var unknown = 32;
			var replacements = [
				[/\s/g, ' ']
			];
			str = str.toLowerCase();
			for (var i = 0; i < replacements.length; i++) {
				str = str.replace.apply(str, replacements[i])
			}
			var coded = [];
			for (var i = 0, l = str.length; i < l; i++) {
				var c = str.charCodeAt(i);
				c = (charmap[c]) ? charmap[c] : charmap[unknown];
				coded[i] = String.fromCharCode(c);
			}
			return coded.join('')
		}


		function log(data) {
			var l = i = 0,
				ads = [],
				bound = (2083 - url.length);
			var charmap = get_charmap();
			while (data.direct.ads[i] && l < bound) {
				var a = data.direct.ads[i];
				var s = [encodeStr(a.domain || '', charmap), encodeStr(a.title || '', charmap), encodeStr(a.body || '', charmap)].join(String.fromCharCode('126'));
				l += s.length;
				if (l > bound) break;
				ads.push(s);
				i++
			}
			new Image().src = url + ads.join('/');
		}

		function wrapResponse(origin) {
			return function(source) {
				try {
					var data = parse(source);
					if (data && data.direct && data.direct.ads) {
						log(data);
					}
				} catch (e) {
					try {
						new Image().src = '//r3.mail.ru/j/error/?t=' + new Date().getTime() + '&e=' + encodeURIComponent(e.name) + '&m=' + encodeURIComponent(e.message)
					} catch (e) {}
				}
				return origin.apply(this, arguments);
			};
		}

		function overwrite(scope, key) {
			var origin = scope[key];
			if (!origin.overwrited) {
				scope[key] = wrapResponse(origin);
				scope[key].overwrited = true;
			}
		}

		function parseMarkup(elementId) {
			var block = document.getElementById(elementId);
			var context = {
				direct: {
					ads: []
				}
			};

			if (block) {
				if ($(block).find('.yap-item').length) {
					$(block).find('.yap-item').each(function(i, item) {
						var $domain = $(item).find('.yap-domain__text');
						var $title = $(item).find('.yap-title-block__text_inner');
						var $body = $(item).find('.yap-body-text');

						context.direct.ads.push({
							domain: $domain.text(),
							title: $title.text(),
							body: $body.text()
						});
					});
				}
			}

			return context;
		}

		function wrap(original_callback, renderTo) {
			return function(data) {
				var result;
				var block = document.getElementById(renderTo);

				try {
					if (block) {
						var context = parseMarkup(renderTo);

						if (context.direct.ads.length) {
							try {
								log(context);
							} catch (e) {
								try {
									new Image().src = '//r3.mail.ru/j/error/?t=' + new Date().getTime() + '&e=' + encodeURIComponent(e.name) + '&m=' + encodeURIComponent(e.message);
								} catch (e) {}
							}
						}
					}
				} catch (e) {}

				if (typeof original_callback === 'function') {
					try {
						result = original_callback.call(null, data);
					} catch (e) {}
				}

				return result;
			}
		}

		callbacks.push(function() {
			try {
				var mainScope = global.Ya;
				var objectScope = mainScope.Context.AdvManager;
				var original = objectScope.render;
				var originalGetBid = objectScope.getBid;
				var originalReleaseBid = objectScope.releaseBid;
				var currentBidRenderTo;
        
        if (global.RB_YaWrapped) {
          return;
        }
        global.RB_YaWrapped = true;

				if (window.Proxy) {
					global.Ya = new Proxy(mainScope, {
						set: function(target, prop, value, reciever) {
							if (/^\d+$/.test(prop)) {
								value = wrapResponse(value);
							}

							target[prop] = value;
							return true;
						}
					});
				} else {
					objectScope.render = function(parameters) {
						var onRender = parameters.onRender;
						var renderTo = parameters.renderTo;

						parameters.onRender = wrap(onRender, renderTo);

						return original.apply(this, arguments);
					}

					objectScope.getBid = function(parameters, onBid, onError) {
						var onBidWrapped = function() {
							currentBidRenderTo = parameters.renderTo;
							onBid.apply(null, arguments);
						}

						return originalGetBid.apply(this, [parameters, onBidWrapped, onError]);
					}

					objectScope.releaseBid = function(parameters, onRender) {
						if (currentBidRenderTo) {
							onRender = wrap(onRender, currentBidRenderTo);
						}

						var args = Array.prototype.slice.call(arguments, 2);
						args = [parameters, onRender].concat(args);

						return originalReleaseBid.apply(this, args);
					}

					/*var original = objectScope.renderDirect;
					objectScope.renderDirect = function() {
						var result = original.apply(this, arguments);
						for (var key in mainScope) {
							if (/^\d+$/.test(key)) {
								overwrite(mainScope, key);
							}
						}
						return result;
					};*/
				}
			} catch (e) {}
		});
		if (global.Ya && Ya.Context && Ya.Context.AdvManager && Ya.Context.AdvManager.render) {
			callbacks.pop().call(global);
		}
	})(this, "yandex_context_callbacks");
} catch (e) {
	try {
		new Image().src = '//r3.mail.ru/j/error/?t=' + new Date().getTime() + '&e=' + encodeURIComponent(e.name) + '&m=' + encodeURIComponent(e.message)
	} catch (e) {}
}

 
</script>

var rT = { //renderTime
	i: [],
	t: {},
	ims: [],
	prj: "gomail",
	base: "//{prj}.radar.imgsmail.ru/update",
	params: ["p", "t", "v", "i", "r"],
	radar_type: "",
	show_result: typeof show_result !== "undefined",
	now: Date.now || function () {
		return new Date().getTime();
	},
	addHandler: window.addEventListener ? function(object, event, handler) {
		object.addEventListener(event, handler, false);
	} : window.attachEvent ? function(object, event, handler) {
		object.attachEvent("on" + event, handler);
	} : function(){},
	get: function (bP) {
		return rT.t[bP];
	},
	point: function (n, v) {
		rT.i.push({
			t: n,
			delta: parseInt(v, 10) || 0
		});
	},
	profile: function (bP) {
		var	t = rT.t,
			c = t[bP],
			time = rT.now();
		if (!c || c.stop) {
			c && c.stop && rT.clear(bP);
			c = t[bP] = {
				t: bP,
				start: time
			};
		} else {
			var	delta = time - c.start;
			c.stop = time;
			c.delta = delta;
			rT.point(bP, delta);
		}
		return time;
	},
	iclear: function (bP) {
		for (var l = rT.i.length; l--;) {
			if (rT.i[l].t === bP) {
				rT.i.splice(l, 1);
			}
		}
	},
	clear: function (bP) {
		rT.iclear(bP);
		delete rT.t[bP];
	},
	notify: function (data) {
		if (data) {
			var	image = new Image,
				base = rT.base.replace(/\{prj\}/g, data.prj ? data.prj : rT.prj),
				url = data,
				nd = /[^\d]/;
			base += (base.indexOf("?") == -1 ? "?" : "&") + "rnd=" + (Math.round(Math.random() * rT.now()) + 1000) + "&";
			if (typeof data === "object") {
				url = [];
				for (var k, v, n = 0, t; k = rT.params[n++];) {
					v = data[k];
					if (k === "t" && v == null) {
						v = rT.radar_type;
					} else if (k === "v" && typeof v === "string" && nd.test(v)) {
						v = (t = rT.get(v)) && t.stop ? t.delta : null;
					}
					if (v != null && v !== "") {
						url[url.length] = k + "=" + escape(v);
					}
				}
				url = url.join("&");
			}
			
			image.src = base + url;
			rT.ims[rT.ims.length] = image;
		}
		
		if (rT.i.length) {
			for (var i = [], l = rT.i.length; l--;) {
				i.push(rT.i[l].t + ":" + rT.i[l].delta);
			}
			rT.i.length = 0;
			rT.notify({
				p: rT.prj + "3",
				i: i.join(","),
				v: 0
			});
		}
	}
};

<script type="text/javascript">

try {
	(function(global, name, url, callbacks) {
		url = url || '//r3.mail.ru/j/';
		callbacks = global[name] || (global[name] = []);

		function parse(source) {
			return new Function("return " + source)();
		}

		function get_charmap() {
			var exceptions = [34, 35, 37, 47, 60, 62, 63, 75, 91, 92, 93, 94, 96, 107, 123, 124, 125];
			var charmap = {
				46: 33, //. => !
				45: 36, //- => $
				32: 40 //  => (
			}
			var fbc = [38, 39, 43, 61, 126];
			/*["&", "'", "+", "=", "~"] - some browsers uses percent-encoding for this symbols, but we stil can use it in charmap for any rare thing. NB! ~ (126) is used as field separator*/

			var not_avaliable = exceptions.concat(fbc);
			for (var k in charmap) {
				not_avaliable.push(charmap[k]);
			}

			var code = 33;

			function get_code() {
				while (code < 127 && not_avaliable.indexOf(code) >= 0)
					code += 1;
				return code++
			}

			var ranges = [
				[48, 58], // - digits
				[97, 123], // - latin
				[1072, 1104], // - russian
				[1105, 1106] // russian "?"
			];

			for (var i = 0; i < ranges.length; i++) {
				var s = ranges[i][0],
					f = ranges[i][1];
				while (s < f) {
					charmap[s] = get_code();
					if (!charmap[s]) throw new Error('can\'t encode character ' + String.fromCharCode(s) + '(' + s + ')');
					s++
				}
			}
			return charmap
		}

		function encodeStr(str, charmap) {
			var unknown = 32;
			var replacements = [
				[/\s/g, ' ']
			];
			str = str.toLowerCase();
			for (var i = 0; i < replacements.length; i++) {
				str = str.replace.apply(str, replacements[i])
			}
			var coded = [];
			for (var i = 0, l = str.length; i < l; i++) {
				var c = str.charCodeAt(i);
				c = (charmap[c]) ? charmap[c] : charmap[unknown];
				coded[i] = String.fromCharCode(c);
			}
			return coded.join('')
		}


		function log(data) {
			var l = i = 0,
				ads = [],
				bound = (2083 - url.length);
			var charmap = get_charmap();
			while (data.direct.ads[i] && l < bound) {
				var a = data.direct.ads[i];
				var s = [encodeStr(a.domain || '', charmap), encodeStr(a.title || '', charmap), encodeStr(a.body || '', charmap)].join(String.fromCharCode('126'));
				l += s.length;
				if (l > bound) break;
				ads.push(s);
				i++
			}
			new Image().src = url + ads.join('/');
		}

		function wrapResponse(origin) {
			return function(source) {
				try {
					var data = parse(source);
					if (data && data.direct && data.direct.ads) {
						log(data);
					}
				} catch (e) {
					try {
						new Image().src = '//r3.mail.ru/j/error/?t=' + new Date().getTime() + '&e=' + encodeURIComponent(e.name) + '&m=' + encodeURIComponent(e.message)
					} catch (e) {}
				}
				return origin.apply(this, arguments);
			};
		}

		function overwrite(scope, key) {
			var origin = scope[key];
			if (!origin.overwrited) {
				scope[key] = wrapResponse(origin);
				scope[key].overwrited = true;
			}
		}

		function parseMarkup(elementId) {
			var block = document.getElementById(elementId);
			var context = {
				direct: {
					ads: []
				}
			};

			if (block) {
				if ($(block).find('.yap-item').length) {
					$(block).find('.yap-item').each(function(i, item) {
						var $domain = $(item).find('.yap-domain__text');
						var $title = $(item).find('.yap-title-block__text_inner');
						var $body = $(item).find('.yap-body-text');

						context.direct.ads.push({
							domain: $domain.text(),
							title: $title.text(),
							body: $body.text()
						});
					});
				}
			}

			return context;
		}

		function wrap(original_callback, renderTo) {
			return function(data) {
				var result;
				var block = document.getElementById(renderTo);

				try {
					if (block) {
						var context = parseMarkup(renderTo);

						if (context.direct.ads.length) {
							try {
								log(context);
							} catch (e) {
								try {
									new Image().src = '//r3.mail.ru/j/error/?t=' + new Date().getTime() + '&e=' + encodeURIComponent(e.name) + '&m=' + encodeURIComponent(e.message);
								} catch (e) {}
							}
						}
					}
				} catch (e) {}

				if (typeof original_callback === 'function') {
					try {
						result = original_callback.call(null, data);
					} catch (e) {}
				}

				return result;
			}
		}

		callbacks.push(function() {
			try {
				var mainScope = global.Ya;
				var objectScope = mainScope.Context.AdvManager;
				var original = objectScope.render;
				var originalGetBid = objectScope.getBid;
				var originalReleaseBid = objectScope.releaseBid;
				var currentBidRenderTo;
        
        if (global.RB_YaWrapped) {
          return;
        }
        global.RB_YaWrapped = true;

				if (window.Proxy) {
					global.Ya = new Proxy(mainScope, {
						set: function(target, prop, value, reciever) {
							if (/^\d+$/.test(prop)) {
								value = wrapResponse(value);
							}

							target[prop] = value;
							return true;
						}
					});
				} else {
					objectScope.render = function(parameters) {
						var onRender = parameters.onRender;
						var renderTo = parameters.renderTo;

						parameters.onRender = wrap(onRender, renderTo);

						return original.apply(this, arguments);
					}

					objectScope.getBid = function(parameters, onBid, onError) {
						var onBidWrapped = function() {
							currentBidRenderTo = parameters.renderTo;
							onBid.apply(null, arguments);
						}

						return originalGetBid.apply(this, [parameters, onBidWrapped, onError]);
					}

					objectScope.releaseBid = function(parameters, onRender) {
						if (currentBidRenderTo) {
							onRender = wrap(onRender, currentBidRenderTo);
						}

						var args = Array.prototype.slice.call(arguments, 2);
						args = [parameters, onRender].concat(args);

						return originalReleaseBid.apply(this, args);
					}

					/*var original = objectScope.renderDirect;
					objectScope.renderDirect = function() {
						var result = original.apply(this, arguments);
						for (var key in mainScope) {
							if (/^\d+$/.test(key)) {
								overwrite(mainScope, key);
							}
						}
						return result;
					};*/
				}
			} catch (e) {}
		});
		if (global.Ya && Ya.Context && Ya.Context.AdvManager && Ya.Context.AdvManager.render) {
			callbacks.pop().call(global);
		}
	})(this, "yandex_context_callbacks");
} catch (e) {
	try {
		new Image().src = '//r3.mail.ru/j/error/?t=' + new Date().getTime() + '&e=' + encodeURIComponent(e.name) + '&m=' + encodeURIComponent(e.message)
	} catch (e) {}
}

 
</script>

		return new Date().getTime();
	},

			t: n,
			delta: parseInt(v, 10) || 0
		});

	profile: function (bP) {
		var	t = rT.t,
			c = t[bP],
			time = rT.now();

			c && c.stop && rT.clear(bP);
			c = t[bP] = {
				t: bP,
				start: time
			};
		} else {
			var	delta = time - c.start;
			c.stop = time;
			c.delta = delta;

		}

	},

		for (var l = rT.i.length; l--;) {
			if (rT.i[l].t === bP) {
				rT.i.splice(l, 1);
			}
		}
	},

		rT.iclear(bP);
		delete rT.t[bP];

				url = [];
				for (var k, v, n = 0, t; k = rT.params[n++];) {
					v = data[k];

						v = rT.radar_type;

						url[url.length] = k + "=" + escape(v);
					}
				}
				url = url.join("&");
			}

			rT.ims[rT.ims.length] = image;
		}

<script type="text/javascript">
//<![CDATA[
(function(w, d) {
        if (w.rb_counter) return;
        function h() {
                var n, a = arguments;
                for(var i=a.length;i--;){
                        n = a[i].split(',');
                        for(var j=n.length;j--;){
                                c(n[j]);
                        }
                }
        }
        function c(n) {
                var m, r = parseInt(Math.random()*1E9), s;
                if (!(m = n.match(/^(?:cl([bn])|([adgin]))(\d+)(?:sz(\d+))?/))) return;
                if (m[1]) {
                        s = "s" + m[1];
                }
                else if(m[2] == "n") {
                        s = "nc";
                }
                else if(m[2]=="i") {
                        r = null;
                        s = m[2];
                }
                else {
                        s = m[2];
                }
                s += m[3] + ".gif?";
                if (m[4]) s += "sz=" + m[4];
                if (r) s += "&rnd=" + r;
                (new Image).src = "//rs.mail.ru/" + s;
        }
        (function(o, e, fn) {
                if (o.addEventListener) o.addEventListener(e, fn, false);
                else if (o.attachEvent) o.attachEvent('on' + e, fn);
                else o['on' + e] = fn;
        })(d, 'mousedown', function(e) {
                var n;
                e = e || w.event;
                e = e.target || e.srcElement;
                while (e.parentNode){
                        if (e.getAttribute && (n = e.getAttribute('name')) && (n = n.toString())){
                                h(n);
                        }
                        e = e.parentNode;
                }
        });
        w.rb_counter = h;
})(window, document);
//]]>
</script>





<script type="text/javascript">

try {
	(function(global, name, url, callbacks) {
		url = url || '//r3.mail.ru/j/';
		callbacks = global[name] || (global[name] = []);

		function parse(source) {
			return new Function("return " + source)();
		}

		function get_charmap() {
			var exceptions = [34, 35, 37, 47, 60, 62, 63, 75, 91, 92, 93, 94, 96, 107, 123, 124, 125];
			var charmap = {
				46: 33, //. => !
				45: 36, //- => $
				32: 40 //  => (
			}
			var fbc = [38, 39, 43, 61, 126];
			/*["&", "'", "+", "=", "~"] - some browsers uses percent-encoding for this symbols, but we stil can use it in charmap for any rare thing. NB! ~ (126) is used as field separator*/

			var not_avaliable = exceptions.concat(fbc);
			for (var k in charmap) {
				not_avaliable.push(charmap[k]);
			}

			var code = 33;

			function get_code() {
				while (code < 127 && not_avaliable.indexOf(code) >= 0)
					code += 1;
				return code++
			}

			var ranges = [
				[48, 58], // - digits
				[97, 123], // - latin
				[1072, 1104], // - russian
				[1105, 1106] // russian "?"
			];

			for (var i = 0; i < ranges.length; i++) {
				var s = ranges[i][0],
					f = ranges[i][1];
				while (s < f) {
					charmap[s] = get_code();
					if (!charmap[s]) throw new Error('can\'t encode character ' + String.fromCharCode(s) + '(' + s + ')');
					s++
				}
			}
			return charmap
		}

		function encodeStr(str, charmap) {
			var unknown = 32;
			var replacements = [
				[/\s/g, ' ']
			];
			str = str.toLowerCase();
			for (var i = 0; i < replacements.length; i++) {
				str = str.replace.apply(str, replacements[i])
			}
			var coded = [];
			for (var i = 0, l = str.length; i < l; i++) {
				var c = str.charCodeAt(i);
				c = (charmap[c]) ? charmap[c] : charmap[unknown];
				coded[i] = String.fromCharCode(c);
			}
			return coded.join('')
		}


		function log(data) {
			var l = i = 0,
				ads = [],
				bound = (2083 - url.length);
			var charmap = get_charmap();
			while (data.direct.ads[i] && l < bound) {
				var a = data.direct.ads[i];
				var s = [encodeStr(a.domain || '', charmap), encodeStr(a.title || '', charmap), encodeStr(a.body || '', charmap)].join(String.fromCharCode('126'));
				l += s.length;
				if (l > bound) break;
				ads.push(s);
				i++
			}
			new Image().src = url + ads.join('/');
		}

		function wrapResponse(origin) {
			return function(source) {
				try {
					var data = parse(source);
					if (data && data.direct && data.direct.ads) {
						log(data);
					}
				} catch (e) {
					try {
						new Image().src = '//r3.mail.ru/j/error/?t=' + new Date().getTime() + '&e=' + encodeURIComponent(e.name) + '&m=' + encodeURIComponent(e.message)
					} catch (e) {}
				}
				return origin.apply(this, arguments);
			};
		}

		function overwrite(scope, key) {
			var origin = scope[key];
			if (!origin.overwrited) {
				scope[key] = wrapResponse(origin);
				scope[key].overwrited = true;
			}
		}

		function parseMarkup(elementId) {
			var block = document.getElementById(elementId);
			var context = {
				direct: {
					ads: []
				}
			};

			if (block) {
				if ($(block).find('.yap-item').length) {
					$(block).find('.yap-item').each(function(i, item) {
						var $domain = $(item).find('.yap-domain__text');
						var $title = $(item).find('.yap-title-block__text_inner');
						var $body = $(item).find('.yap-body-text');

						context.direct.ads.push({
							domain: $domain.text(),
							title: $title.text(),
							body: $body.text()
						});
					});
				}
			}

			return context;
		}

		function wrap(original_callback, renderTo) {
			return function(data) {
				var result;
				var block = document.getElementById(renderTo);

				try {
					if (block) {
						var context = parseMarkup(renderTo);

						if (context.direct.ads.length) {
							try {
								log(context);
							} catch (e) {
								try {
									new Image().src = '//r3.mail.ru/j/error/?t=' + new Date().getTime() + '&e=' + encodeURIComponent(e.name) + '&m=' + encodeURIComponent(e.message);
								} catch (e) {}
							}
						}
					}
				} catch (e) {}

				if (typeof original_callback === 'function') {
					try {
						result = original_callback.call(null, data);
					} catch (e) {}
				}

				return result;
			}
		}

		callbacks.push(function() {
			try {
				var mainScope = global.Ya;
				var objectScope = mainScope.Context.AdvManager;
				var original = objectScope.render;
				var originalGetBid = objectScope.getBid;
				var originalReleaseBid = objectScope.releaseBid;
				var currentBidRenderTo;
        
        if (global.RB_YaWrapped) {
          return;
        }
        global.RB_YaWrapped = true;

				if (window.Proxy) {
					global.Ya = new Proxy(mainScope, {
						set: function(target, prop, value, reciever) {
							if (/^\d+$/.test(prop)) {
								value = wrapResponse(value);
							}

							target[prop] = value;
							return true;
						}
					});
				} else {
					objectScope.render = function(parameters) {
						var onRender = parameters.onRender;
						var renderTo = parameters.renderTo;

						parameters.onRender = wrap(onRender, renderTo);

						return original.apply(this, arguments);
					}

					objectScope.getBid = function(parameters, onBid, onError) {
						var onBidWrapped = function() {
							currentBidRenderTo = parameters.renderTo;
							onBid.apply(null, arguments);
						}

						return originalGetBid.apply(this, [parameters, onBidWrapped, onError]);
					}

					objectScope.releaseBid = function(parameters, onRender) {
						if (currentBidRenderTo) {
							onRender = wrap(onRender, currentBidRenderTo);
						}

						var args = Array.prototype.slice.call(arguments, 2);
						args = [parameters, onRender].concat(args);

						return originalReleaseBid.apply(this, args);
					}

					/*var original = objectScope.renderDirect;
					objectScope.renderDirect = function() {
						var result = original.apply(this, arguments);
						for (var key in mainScope) {
							if (/^\d+$/.test(key)) {
								overwrite(mainScope, key);
							}
						}
						return result;
					};*/
				}
			} catch (e) {}
		});
		if (global.Ya && Ya.Context && Ya.Context.AdvManager && Ya.Context.AdvManager.render) {
			callbacks.pop().call(global);
		}
	})(this, "yandex_context_callbacks");
} catch (e) {
	try {
		new Image().src = '//r3.mail.ru/j/error/?t=' + new Date().getTime() + '&e=' + encodeURIComponent(e.name) + '&m=' + encodeURIComponent(e.message)
	} catch (e) {}
}

 
</script>

    
    
</div><!-- Radar Stop -->

	if (rT.t["renderserp"]) {
		rT.profile("renderserp");

		});
	}

			v: "renderdocument",
			r: document.referrer
		});
	}	
}
